**7 Q-OPEN RESOLVED V1 enumerate:**

1. **В§3.1 Q-OPEN-1 Versioning/migration** вҖ” Migration Runner orchestrator-level pre-pipeline Г®n `contextBuilder.js` (D2 thin scope preserved); ADR 018 В§4 alignment confirm
2. **В§3.2 Q-OPEN-2 Layer D вүӨ50ms enforcement** вҖ” V1 sync Promise.race timeout (current `budget.js`) + `BUDGET_EXCEEDED` severity 'soft' default; V1.5 AbortController trigger cГўnd Faza 3 batch 1 вүҘ1 engine reproducibly p95 >50ms
3. **В§3.3 Q-OPEN-3 Observability granularity** вҖ” Aggregate orchestrator-level (1 CDL `pipeline_event` + `subSpans[]` array) per session-tick; per-adapter Sentry only on err. ADR 011 В§X amendment defining payload schema applied
4. **В§3.4 Q-OPEN-4 Pipeline ordering** вҖ” SEQUENTIAL STRICT preserved per ADR 026 В§1.10 LOCKED + `runPipeline` for-await sequential current `5a16550`; V1.5 parallel-where-safe trigger В§5.6 threshold preserved
5. **В§3.5 Q-OPEN-5 State source resolution** вҖ” Hierarchical fallback Tier 1 IndexedDB primary вҶ’ Tier 0 ephemeral вҶ’ Tier 2 Firestore async background (NEVER pipeline blocking); silent degradation default per ADR 025
6. **В§3.6 Q-OPEN-6 Error recovery semantics** вҖ” HYBRID per error code taxonomy + D4 amendment additive `AdapterError.severity: 'soft' | 'hard'` field (default `'hard'` fail-safe Anti-Cascade Silent). Resolves ADR 025 graceful vs ADR_CASCADE_DEFENSE_v1 strict tension. `runPipeline` policy-aware halt logic implemented
7. **В§3.7 Q-OPEN-7 Convergence Guard tier downgrade** вҖ” Batch periodic per session-end (NOT per-session-tick) + cooldown asymmetric (T0вҶ’T1вҶ’T2 instant, T2вҶ’T1/T1вҶ’T0 cooldown 7 zile + N=3 consecutive sessions per ADR 009 В§AMENDMENT)

**D4 amendment additive `severity` field LOCKED V1:** `AdapterError` envelope additive optional `severity: 'soft' | 'hard'` field. Default `'hard'` if absent (fail-safe Bugatti craft). Severity-aware policy `runPipeline`: 'soft' вҶ’ continue-graceful (ADR 025 alignment); 'hard' вҶ’ halt-strict (Anti-Cascade Silent alignment). Concrete engine severity mapping per ADR 026 В§9.1-В§9.8 (Periodization stale CDL вҶ’ 'hard'; Tempo/Bayesian/Specialization/Warm-up/Deload data degradation вҶ’ 'soft'; Goal Adaptation phase ambiguous вҶ’ 'soft'; Energy Adjustment emoji absent вҶ’ 'soft').
